18. **[è‹±ä¼Ÿè¾¾ä¸è”æƒ³å®£å¸ƒæœ€æ–°åˆä½œè®¡åˆ’ï¼šè”æƒ³äººå·¥æ™ºèƒ½äº‘è¶…çº§å·¥å‚](https://finance.sina.com.cn/hy/hyjz/2026-01-07/doc-inhfmtvu5306076.shtml)**
   - ğŸ“° æ¥æº: æ–°æµªè´¢ç»

   - ğŸ’¬ ç®€ä»‹: è”æƒ³ä¸è‹±ä¼Ÿè¾¾åˆä½œå…±å»ºäººå·¥æ™ºèƒ½äº‘è¶…çº§å·¥å‚ï¼Œèšç„¦AIæ¨¡å‹è®­ç»ƒä¸­çš„â€œtime to first tokenâ€æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–ï¼Œä¾æ‰˜NVIDIA Vera Rubinå¹³å°æå‡AIæ¨ç†æ•ˆç‡ã€‚è¯¥åˆä½œå¼ºåŒ–äº†AIèŠ¯ç‰‡ä¸äº‘æœåŠ¡åœ¨ä¼ä¸šçº§åœºæ™¯ä¸­çš„ååŒèƒ½åŠ›ï¼Œæ¨åŠ¨AIåº”ç”¨åœ¨å¤šè®¾å¤‡ç”Ÿæ€ä¸­çš„è½åœ°ä¸æ¼”è¿›ã€‚


### è®¡ç®—æœºè§†è§‰

1. **[AI-native robotic vision systems enabled by in-sensor computing](https://www.nature.com/articles/s44335-025-00047-z)**
   - ğŸ“° æ¥æº: Nature
   - ğŸ•’ å‘å¸ƒæ—¶é—´: 2026å¹´01æœˆ07æ—¥
   - â­ è¯„åˆ†: 9.5/10
   - ğŸ’¬ ç®€ä»‹: AI-native robotic vision systems leverage in-sensor spike encoding to convert optical stimuli into discrete spike trains, enabling energy-efficient and noise-resistant visual processing. This spike-based approach aligns with spiking neural network (SNN) architectures, offering superior computational efficiency and low-latency event-driven detection for real-time robotic perception. The technology supports dynamic motion interpretation with minimal power consumption in autonomous vision tasks.
